Header for the enumerated pixel format definitions.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{begin__code_8h_aa4c7a931f4a968f818b2a1b10a432185}{D\+E\+C\+L\+S\+P\+EC}} int \mbox{\hyperlink{begin__code_8h_a81faf4ba0455dc75f2e0507eddb79401}{S\+D\+L\+C\+A\+LL}} S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Palette\+Colors (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_s_d_l___palette}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Palette}} $\ast$}]{palette,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_s_d_l___color}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Color}} $\ast$}]{colors,  }\item[{int}]{firstcolor,  }\item[{int}]{ncolors }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set a range of colors in a palette. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em palette} & The palette to modify. \\
\hline
{\em colors} & An array of colors to copy into the palette. \\
\hline

\hline
{\em ncolors} & The number of entries to modify.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
